<Scene Heading>EXT. STRATOSPHERE - DAY</Scene Heading>

<NARRATIVE>The glory of stratospheric dawn.  The engines of a silver Lockheed U-2F rasp upon the trace oxygen here at 72,500 feet.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>Scattered cloud formations hang over the blue brilliance of sea far, far below.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>In the haze, the looming edge of land.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>SUPER: FLIGHT G-3101. OCTOBER 14TH, 1962. OVER CUBA.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>The spy plane's CAMERA DOORS whine open.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>The glassy eye of the 36-inch camera focuses.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>And then with a BANGBANGBANGBANG, its high-speed motor kicks in, shutter flying.</NARRATIVE>
